# <a name="excel-javascript-api-requirement-sets"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-102">Excel JavaScript API 要求集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-102">Excel JavaScript API requirement sets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-p101">要求集是指各组已命名的 API 成员。Office 加载项使用清单中指定的要求集或执行运行时检查，以确定 Office 主机是否支持加载项所需的 API。有关详细信息，请参阅 [Office 版本和要求集](/office/dev/add-ins/develop/office-versions-and-requirement-sets)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-p101">Requirement sets are named groups of API members. Office Add-ins use requirement sets specified in the manifest or use a runtime check to determine whether an Office host supports APIs that an add-in needs. For more information, see [Office versions and requirement sets](/office/dev/add-ins/develop/office-versions-and-requirement-sets).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-p102">Excel 加载项跨多个版本 Office 运行，包括 Windows 版 Office 2016 或更高版本、Office 网页版、Mac 版 Office 和 iPad 版 Office。下表列出了 Excel 要求集、支持各个要求集的 Office 主机应用程序，以及这些应用程序的内部版本或生成号。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-p102">Excel add-ins run across multiple versions of Office, including Office 2016 or later on Windows, Office for iPad, Office for Mac, and Office Online. The following table lists the Excel requirement sets, the Office host applications that support each requirement set, and the build versions or number for those applications.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="617de-108">若要在任何编号的要求集中使用 API，你应该引用 CDN 上的**生产**库：https://appsforoffice.microsoft.com/lib/1/hosted/office.js。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-108">To use APIs in any of the numbered requirement sets, you should reference the **production** library on the CDN: https://appsforoffice.microsoft.com/lib/1/hosted/office.js.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="617de-109">有关使用预览 API 的信息，请参阅本文的 [Excel JavaScript 预览 API](#excel-javascript-preview-apis) 部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-109">For information about using preview APIs, see the [Excel JavaScript preview APIs](#excel-javascript-preview-apis) section within this article.</span></span>

## <a name="excel-javascript-preview-apis"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-200">Excel JavaScript 预览 API</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-200">Excel JavaScript preview APIs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-201">新的 Excel JavaScript API 首先在“预览版”中引入，在进行充分测试并获得用户反馈后，它将成为编号的特定要求集的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-201">New Excel JavaScript APIs are first introduced in "preview" and later become part of a specific, numbered requirement set after sufficient testing occurs and user feedback is acquired.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-202">第一个表提供了 API 的简明摘要，而后续表提供了详细列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-202">The first table provides a concise summary of the APIs, while the subsequent table gives a detailed list.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="617de-203">预览 API 可能会发生变更，不适合在生产环境中使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-203">Preview APIs are subject to change and are not intended for use in a production environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-204">我们建议你仅在测试和开发环境中试用它们。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-204">We recommend that you try them out in test and development environments only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-205">不要在生产环境或业务关键型文档中使用预览 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-205">Do not use preview APIs in a production environment or within business-critical documents.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="617de-206">若要使用预览 API，你必须引用 CDN 上的 **beta** 库（https://appsforoffice.microsoft.com/lib/beta/hosted/office.js)并且你可能还需要加入 Office 预览体验成员计划才能获得新的 Office 版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-206">To use preview APIs, you must reference the **beta** library on the CDN (https://appsforoffice.microsoft.com/lib/beta/hosted/office.js) and you may also need to join the Office Insider program to get a recent Office build.</span></span>

## <a name="whats-new-in-excel-javascript-api-19"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-632">Excel JavaScript API 1.9 的最近更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-632">What’s new in Excel JavaScript API 1.9</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-633">超过 500 个新  Excel API 随 1.9 要求集一起推出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-633">More than 500 new Excel APIs were introduced with the 1.9 requirement set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-634">第一个表提供了 API 的简明摘要，而后续表提供了详细列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-634">The first table provides a concise summary of the APIs, while the subsequent table gives a detailed list.</span></span>

## <a name="whats-new-in-excel-javascript-api-18"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-1994">Excel JavaScript API 1.8 的最近更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-1994">What’s new in Excel JavaScript API 1.8</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-1995">Excel JavaScript API 要求集 1.8 的功能包括适用于数据透视表、数据验证、图表、图表事件、性能选项和工作簿创建的 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-1995">The Excel JavaScript API requirement set 1.8 features include APIs for PivotTables, data validation, charts, events for charts, performance options, and workbook creation.</span></span>

### <a name="pivottable"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-1996">数据透视表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-1996">PivotTable</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-1997">加载项通过数据透视表 API 的波形 2 设置数据透视表的层次结构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-1997">Wave 2 of the PivotTable APIs lets add-ins set the hierarchies of a PivotTable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-1998">现在可以控制数据及其聚合方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-1998">You can now control the data and how it is aggregated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-1999">[数据透视表](/office/dev/add-ins/excel/excel-add-ins-pivottables)一文详细介绍了新的数据透视表功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-1999">Our [PivotTable article](/office/dev/add-ins/excel/excel-add-ins-pivottables) has more on the new PivotTable functionality.</span></span>

### <a name="data-validation"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-2000">数据有效性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-2000">Data Validation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-2001">数据有效性可以控制用户在工作表中输入的内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-2001">Data validation gives you control of what a user enters in a worksheet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-2002">可以将单元格限制为预定义的答案集，或者在用户输入无效数据时提供弹出警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-2002">You can limit cells to pre-defined answer sets or give pop-up warnings about undesirable input.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-2003">立即详细了解[向区域添加数据有效性](/office/dev/add-ins/excel/excel-add-ins-data-validation)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-2003">Learn more about [adding data validation to ranges](/office/dev/add-ins/excel/excel-add-ins-data-validation) today.</span></span>

### <a name="charts"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-2004">图表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-2004">Charts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-2005">另一轮图表 API 可更好地对图表元素进行编程控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-2005">Another round of Chart APIs brings even greater programmatic control over chart elements.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-2006">现在，你对图例、坐标轴、趋势线和绘图区拥有更高的访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-2006">You now have greater access to the legend, axes, trendline, and plot area.</span></span>

### <a name="events"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-2007">事件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-2007">Events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-2008">已为图表添加更多[事件](/office/dev/add-ins/excel/excel-add-ins-events)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-2008">More [events](/office/dev/add-ins/excel/excel-add-ins-events) have been added for charts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-2009">让加载项处理用于与图表的交互。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-2009">Have your add-in react to users interacting with the chart.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-2010">此外，你还可以在整个工作簿中[触发事件](/office/dev/add-ins/excel/performance#enable-and-disable-events)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-2010">You can also [toggle events](/office/dev/add-ins/excel/performance#enable-and-disable-events) firing across the entire workbook.</span></span>

## <a name="whats-new-in-excel-javascript-api-17"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-3064">Excel JavaScript API 1.7 的最近更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3064">What's new in Excel JavaScript API 1.7</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-3065">Excel JavaScript API 要求集 1.7 的功能包括用于图表、事件、工作表、区域、文档属性、已命名项目、保护选项和样式的 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3065">The Excel JavaScript API requirement set 1.7 features include APIs for charts, events, worksheets, ranges, document properties, named items, protection options and styles.</span></span>

### <a name="customize-charts"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-3066">自定义图表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3066">Customize charts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-3067">通过新的图表 API，你可以创建其他图表类型、向图表中添加数据系列、设置图表标题、添加轴标题、添加显示单位、添加采用移动平均值的趋势线、将趋势线更改为线性趋势线等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3067">With the new chart APIs, you can create additional chart types, add a data series to a chart, set the chart title, add an axis title, add display unit, add a trendline with moving average, change a trendline to linear, and more.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-3068">下面是一些示例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3068">The following are some examples:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3069">图表轴 - 获取、设置、格式化和删除图表中的轴单位、标签和标题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3069">Chart axis - get, set, format and remove axis unit, label and title in a chart.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3070">图表系列 - 添加、设置和删除图表中的某个系列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3070">Chart series - add, set, and delete a series in a chart.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="617de-3071">更改系列标记、绘制顺序和大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3071">Change series markers, plot orders and sizing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3072">图表趋势线 - 添加、获取和格式化图表中的趋势线。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3072">Chart trendlines - add, get, and format trendlines in a chart.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3073">图表图例 - 设置图表中的图例字体的格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3073">Chart legend - format the legend font in a chart.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3074">图表点 - 设置图表点颜色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3074">Chart point - set chart point color.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3075">图表标题子字符串 - 获取和设置图表的标题子字符串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3075">Chart title substring -  get and set title substring for a chart.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3076">图表类型 - 用于创建更多图表类型的选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3076">Chart type - option to create more chart types.</span></span>

### <a name="events"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-3077">事件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3077">Events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-3078">Excel 事件 API 提供了多个事件处理程序，以便加载项能够在发生特定事件时自动运行指定的函数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3078">Excel events APIs provide a variety of event handlers that allow your add-in to automatically run a designated function when a specific event occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-3079">可以将函数设计为执行方案所需的任何操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3079">You can design that function to perform whatever actions your scenario requires.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-3080">有关当前可用的事件列表，请参阅[使用 Excel JavaScript API 处理事件](/office/dev/add-ins/excel/excel-add-ins-events)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3080">For a list of events that are currently available, see [Work with Events using the Excel JavaScript API](/office/dev/add-ins/excel/excel-add-ins-events).</span></span>

### <a name="customize-the-appearance-of-worksheets-and-ranges"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-3081">自定义工作表和区域的外观</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3081">Customize the appearance of worksheets and ranges</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-3082">使用新的 API 可以通过多种方式自定义工作表的外观：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3082">Using the new APIs, you can customize the appearance of worksheets in multiple ways:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3083">冻结窗格，使特定行或列在你滚动工作表时保持可见。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3083">Freeze panes to keep specific rows or columns visible when you scroll in the worksheet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-3084">例如，如果工作表中的第一行包含标题，则可以冻结此行，以便在你向下滚动工作表时列标题保持可见。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3084">For example, if the first row in your worksheet contains headers, you might freeze that row so that the column headers will remain visible as you scroll down the worksheet.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3085">修改工作表标签颜色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3085">Modify the worksheet tab color.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3086">添加工作表标题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3086">Add worksheet headings.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="617de-3087">可以通过多种方式自定义区域的外观：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3087">You can customize the appearance of ranges in multiple ways:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3088">设置某个区域的单元格样式，确保该区域内的所有单元格采用一致的格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3088">Set the cell style for a range to ensure sure that all cells in the range have consistent formatting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-3089">单元格 样式是一组定义的格式特征，例如字体和字号、数字格式、单元格边框和单元格底纹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3089">A cell style is a defined set of formatting characteristics, such as fonts and font sizes, number formats, cell borders, and cell shading.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-3090">使用 Excel 中的任意内置单元格样式，或者使用自己的自定义单元格样式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3090">Use any of Excel's built-in cell styles or create your own custom cell style.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3091">设置区域的文本方向。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3091">Set the text orientation for a range.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3092">添加或修改区域上链接至工作表中的其他位置或外部位置的超链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3092">Add or modify a hyperlink on a range that links to another location in the workbook or to an external location.</span></span>

### <a name="manage-document-properties"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-3093">管理文档属性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3093">Manage document properties</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-3094">使用文档属性 API，你可以访问内置文档属性，并且还可以创建和管理自定义文档属性，以存储工作表的状态和驱动工作流和业务逻辑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3094">Using the document properties APIs, you can access built-in document properties and also create and manage custom document properties to store state of the workbook and drive workflow and business logic.</span></span>

### <a name="copy-worksheets"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-3095">复制工作表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3095">Copy worksheets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-3096">使用工作表复制 APIs，你可以将一个工作表中的数据和格式复制到相同工作簿中的另一个工作表，从而减少所需的数据传输量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3096">Using the worksheet copy APIs, you can copy the data and format from one worksheet to a new worksheet within the same workbook and reduce the amount of data transfer needed.</span></span>

### <a name="handle-ranges-with-ease"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-3097">轻松地处理区域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3097">Handle ranges with ease</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-3098">使用各种区域 API，你可以完成诸如获取周围区域、获取大小经过重设的区域之类的任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3098">Using the various range APIs, you can do things such as get the surrounding region, get a resized range, and more.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-3099">这些 API 可以显著提高诸如区域操作和寻址之类任务的效率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3099">These APIs should make tasks like range manipulation and addressing much more efficient.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-3100">此外：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3100">In addition:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3101">工作簿和工作表保护选项 - 使用这些 API 可保护工作表和工作簿结构中的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3101">Workbook and worksheet protection options - use these APIs to protect data in a worksheet and the workbook structure.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3102">更新已命名项目 - 使用此 API 可更新已命名项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3102">Update a named item - use this API to update a named item.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-3103">获取活动单元格 - 使用此 API 可获取工作表中的活动单元格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-3103">Get active cell  - use this API to get the active cell of a workbook.</span></span>

## <a name="whats-new-in-excel-javascript-api-16"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-4176">Excel JavaScript API 1.6 的最近更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4176">What's new in Excel JavaScript API 1.6</span></span> 

### <a name="conditional-formatting"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-4177">条件格式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4177">Conditional formatting</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-4178">引入了区域的条件格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4178">Introduces conditional formating of a range.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-4179">允许以下条件格式类型：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4179">Allows the following types of conditional formatting:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4180">色阶</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4180">Color scale</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4181">数据栏</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4181">Data bar</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4182">图标集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4182">Icon set</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4183">自定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4183">Custom</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-4184">此外：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4184">In addition:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4185">返回应用条件格式的区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4185">Returns the range the conditional format is applied to.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4186">删除条件格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4186">Removal of conditional formatting.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4187">提供优先级和 stopifTrue 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4187">Provides priority and stopifTrue capability.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4188">获取给定区域内所有条件格式的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4188">Get collection of all conditional formatting on a given range.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4189">清除当前指定区域中处于活动状态的所有条件格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4189">Clears all conditional formats active on the current specified range.</span></span>

##  <a name="whats-new-in-excel-javascript-api-15"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-4709">Excel JavaScript API 1.5 的最近更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4709">What's new in Excel JavaScript API 1.5</span></span>

### <a name="custom-xml-part"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-4710">自定义 XML 部件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4710">Custom XML part</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4711">将自定义 XML 部件集合添加到工作簿对象中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4711">Addition of custom XML parts collection to workbook object.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4712">使用 ID 获取自定义 XML 部件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4712">Get custom XML part using ID</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4713">获取其命名空间匹配给定命名空间的自定义 XML 部件的新作用域内集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4713">Get a new scoped collection of custom XML parts whose namespaces match the given namespace.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4714">获取与某个部件关联的 XML 字符串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4714">Get XML string associated with a part.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4715">提供部件的 ID 和命名空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4715">Provide id and namespace of a part.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4716">向工作簿添加新的自定义 XML 部件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4716">Adds a new custom XML part to the workbook.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4717">设置整个 XML 部件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4717">Set entire XML part.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4718">删除自定义 XML 部件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4718">Delete a custom XML part.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4719">删除其给定名称来自由 xpath 标识的元素的属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4719">Delete an attribute with the given name from the element identified by xpath.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4720">按 xpath 查询 XML 内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4720">Query the XML content by xpath.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4721">插入、更新和删除属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4721">Insert, update and delete attribute.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-4722">**参考实现：** 请参阅[此处](https://github.com/mandren/Excel-CustomXMLPart-Demo)，了解说明如何在外接程序中使用自定义 XML 部件的参考实现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4722">**Reference implementation:** Please refer [here](https://github.com/mandren/Excel-CustomXMLPart-Demo) for a reference implementation that shows how custom XML parts can be used in an add-in.</span></span>

### <a name="others"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-4723">其他</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4723">Others</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-p637">`range.getSurroundingRegion()` 返回一个 Range 对象，该对象表示此范围的周围区域。周围区域是由相对于该范围的空白行和空白列的任何组合所限定的范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-p637">`range.getSurroundingRegion()` Returns a Range object that represents the surrounding region for this range. A surrounding region is a range bounded by any combination of blank rows and blank columns relative to this range.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4726">对表列执行 `getNextColumn()`、`getPreviousColumn()` 以及 \`getLast() 操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4726">`getNextColumn()` and `getPreviousColumn()`, \`getLast() on table column.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4727">对工作簿执行 `getActiveWorksheet()` 操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4727">`getActiveWorksheet()` on the workbook.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4728">工作簿的 `getRange(address: string)` 关闭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4728">`getRange(address: string)` off of workbook.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-p638">`getBoundingRange(ranges: )` 获取包含提供的范围的最小 range 对象。例如，介于 “B2:C5” 和 “D10:E15” 之间的边界范围为 “B2:E15”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-p638">`getBoundingRange(ranges: )` Gets the smallest range object that encompasses the provided ranges. For example, the bounding range between "B2:C5" and "D10:E15" is "B2:E15".</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4731">对各种集合（例如已命名项目、工作表、表等）执行 `getCount()` 操作以获取集合中的项目数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4731">`getCount()` on various collections such as named item, worksheet, table, etc. to get number of items in a collection.</span></span> `workbook.worksheets.getCount()`
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4732">对各种集合（如工作表、表列、图标点、范围视图集合）执行 `getFirst()` 和 `getLast()` 以及 get last 操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4732">`getFirst()` and `getLast()` and get last on various collection such as tworksheet, able column, chart points, range view collection.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4733">对工作表、表列集合执行 `getNext()` 和 `getPrevious()` 操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4733">`getNext()` and `getPrevious()` on worksheet, table column collection.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4734">`getRangeR1C1()` 获取以特定行索引和列索引开始并跨越了一定数量的行和列的 range 对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4734">`getRangeR1C1()` Gets the range object beginning at a particular row index and column index, and spanning a certain number of rows and columns.</span></span>

## <a name="whats-new-in-excel-javascript-api-14"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-4844">Excel JavaScript API 1.4 的最近更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4844">What's new in Excel JavaScript API 1.4</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="617de-4845">下面介绍了要求集 1.4 中 Excel JavaScript API 的新增内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4845">The following are the new additions to the Excel JavaScript APIs in requirement set 1.4.</span></span>

### <a name="named-item-add-and-new-properties"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-4846">添加了已命名项和新属性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4846">Named item add and new properties</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-4847">新属性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4847">New properties:</span></span>

* `comment`
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4848">`scope`：限定到工作表或工作簿的项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4848">`scope` worksheet or workbook scoped items</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4849">`worksheet`：返回已命名项限定到的工作表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4849">`worksheet` returns the worksheet on which the named item is scoped to.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-4850">新方法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4850">New methods:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4851">`add(name: string, reference: Range or string, comment: string)`：将新名称添加到给定范围的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4851">`add(name: string, reference: Range or string, comment: string)`Adds a new name to the collection of the given scope.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4852">`addFormulaLocal(name: string, formula: string, comment: string)`：使用用户的公式区域设置，将新名称添加到给定范围的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4852">`addFormulaLocal(name: string, formula: string, comment: string)` Adds a new name to the collection of the given scope using the user's locale for the formula.</span></span>

### <a name="settings-api-in-the-excel-namespace"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-4853">Excel 命名空间中的设置 API</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4853">Settings API in the Excel namespace</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-4854">[Setting](/javascript/api/excel/excel.setting) 对象表示文档保留设置的键值对。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4854">The [Setting](/javascript/api/excel/excel.setting) object represents a key:value pair for a setting persisted to the document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="617de-4855">`Excel.Setting` 的功能等同于 `Office.Settings`，但使用批处理 API 语法，而不是通用 API 的回调模型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4855">The functionality of `Excel.Setting` is equivalent to `Office.Settings`, but uses the batched API syntax, rather than the Common API's callback model.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="617de-4856">API 包括通过键获取设置条目的 `getItem()`，以及将指定键值设置对添加到工作簿的 `add()`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4856">APIs include `getItem()` to get setting entry via the key, `add()` to add the specified key:value setting pair to the workbook.</span></span>

### <a name="others"></a><span data-ttu-id="617de-4857">其他</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4857">Others</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4858">设置表列名称（旧版只允许读取）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4858">Set table column name (prior version only allows reading).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4859">将表列添加到表的末尾（旧版只允许添加到除末尾之外的其他任何位置）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4859">Add table column to the end of the table (prior version only allows anywhere but last).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4860">一次性向表中添加多行（旧版只允许一次添加 1 行）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4860">Add multiple rows to a table at a time (prior version only allows 1 row at a time).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-4861">`range.getColumnsAfter(count: number)` 和 `range.getColumnsBefore(count: number)` 分别用于获取当前 Range 对象的右/左侧的一定数量的列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-4861">`range.getColumnsAfter(count: number)` and `range.getColumnsBefore(count: number)` to get a certain number of columns to the right/left of the current Range object.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="617de-p649">获取项或 NULL 对象函数：此功能允许使用键获取对象。如果没有对象，返回的对象的 isNullObject 属性为 true。这样一来，开发者可以检查对象是否存在，而无需通过异常处理来进行处理。适用于工作表、已命名项、绑定、图表系列等</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="617de-p649">Get item or null object function: This functionality allows getting object using a key. If the object does not exist, the returned object's isNullObject property will be true. This alows developers to check if an object exists or not without having to handle it thorugh exception handling. Available on worksheet, named-item, binding, chart series, etc.</span></span>

    ```javascript
    worksheet.GetItemOrNullObject()
    ```
